>> Issue: [B815:write] os.write
   Severity: High   Confidence: Medium
   Location: /home/blue/PyPIAgent/Dataset/study/unzip_benign/metaflow-2.15.7/metaflow-2.15.7/metaflow/plugins/env_escape/__init__.py:107
   More Info: https://bandit.readthedocs.io/en/latest/plugins/b815_write.html
106	                        ) as f:
107	                            f.write(
108	                                """
109	import importlib
110	import os
111	import sys
112	from metaflow.plugins.env_escape.client_modules import ModuleImporter
113	from metaflow.metaflow_config import ESCAPE_HATCH_WARNING
114	
115	# This is a trampoline file to ensure that the ModuleImporter to handle the emulated
116	# modules gets properly loaded. If multiple modules are emulated by a single configuration
117	# the first import will cause this trampoline file to be loaded. All other calls will use
118	# the module importer since we insert the importer at the head of the meta_path
119	
120	def load():
121	    # We check if we are not overriding a module that already exists; to do so, we remove
122	    # the path we live at from sys.path and check
123	    old_paths = sys.path
124	    cur_path = os.path.dirname(__file__)
125	    sys.path = [p for p in old_paths if p != cur_path]
126	    # Handle special case where we launch a shell (including with a command)
127	    # and we are in the CWD (searched if '' is present in sys.path)
128	    if cur_path == os.getcwd() and '' in sys.path:
129	        sys.path.remove("")
130	
131	    # Remove the module (this file) to reload it properly. Do *NOT* update sys.modules but
132	    # modify directly since it may be referenced elsewhere
133	    del sys.modules["{module_name}"]
134	
135	    for prefix in {prefixes}:
136	        try:
137	            importlib.import_module(prefix)
138	        except ImportError:
139	            # Here we actually have two cases: we are being imported from the client (inner env)
140	            # in which case we are happy (since no module exists) OR we are being imported by the
141	            # server in which case we could not find the underlying module so we re-raise
142	            # this error.
143	            # We distinguish these cases by checking if the executable is the
144	            # python_executable the server should be using
145	            if sys.executable == "{python_executable}":
146	                raise
147	            # print("Env escape using executable {python_executable}")
148	        else:
149	            # Inverse logic as above here.
150	            if sys.executable != "{python_executable}" and ESCAPE_HATCH_WARNING:
151	                # We use the package locally and warn user.
152	                print("Not using environment escape for '%s' as module present" % prefix)
153	            # In both cases, we don't load our loader since
154	            # the package is locally present
155	            sys.path = old_paths
156	            return
157	    sys.path = old_paths
158	    m = ModuleImporter("{python_executable}", "{pythonpath}", {max_pickle_version}, "{path}", {prefixes})
159	    sys.meta_path.insert(0, m)
160	    # Reload this module using the ModuleImporter
161	    importlib.import_module("{module_name}")
162	
163	if not "{python_executable}":
164	    raise RuntimeError(
165	        "Trying to access an escaped module ({module_name}) without a valid interpreter")
166	load()
167	""".format(
168	                                    python_executable=ENV_ESCAPE_PY,
169	                                    pythonpath=ENV_ESCAPE_PATHS,
170	                                    max_pickle_version=int(ENV_ESCAPE_PICKLE_VERSION),
171	                                    path=path,
172	                                    prefixes=module_names,
173	                                    module_name=module_name,
174	                                )
